<td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">函数执行的结果状态。执行成功返回OH_NN_SUCCESS；失败返回具体错误码，具体失败错误码可参考<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/capi-neural-network-runtime-type-h#oh_nn_returncode">OH_NN_ReturnCode</a>。</td> </tr>  </tbody></table></div> </div> </div> <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 1015px;"><h3 id="oh_nntensordesc_getbytesize" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet">OH_NNTensorDesc_GetByteSize()<i class="anchor-icon _ngcontent-lhx-c106="" class="handle-button copy-button"><div _ngcontent-lhx-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">复制</div></div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lhx-c106="" class="highlight-scroll-div"><pre class="hljs-title">OH_NNTensorDesc_GetByteSize</span><span class="hljs-params">(<span class="hljs-type">const</span> NN_TensorDesc *tensorDesc, <span class="hljs-type">size_t</span> href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/capi-neuralnetworkruntime-nn-tensordesc">NN_TensorDesc</a>的形状和数据类型计算得到的数据占用字节数。</p> *byteSize</td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">返回的数据字节数。</td> </tr>  </tbody></table></div> </div> <p><strong>返回：</strong></p>  <div class="tablenoborder"><div class="tbBox"><table <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 1135px;"><h3 id="oh_nntensor_create" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet">OH_NNTensor_Create()<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="oh_nntensor_create" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3><div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span></div><div _ngcontent-lhx-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-lhx-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-lhx-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-lhx-c106="" class="handle-button expand-button"><div _ngcontent-lhx-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">收起</div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lhx-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-right"><div _ngcontent-lhx-c106="" class="handle-button ai-button"></div><div _ngcontent-lhx-c106="" class="handle-button line-button"><div _ngcontent-lhx-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">自动换行</div></div><div _ngcontent-lhx-c106="" class="handle-button theme-button"><div _ngcontent-lhx-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">深色代码主题</div></div><div _ngcontent-lhx-c106="" class="handle-button copy-button"><div _ngcontent-lhx-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">复制</div></div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lhx-c106="" class="highlight-scroll-div"><pre class="screen prettyprint linenums hljs language-scss" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li>NN_Tensor *<span class="hljs-built_in">OH_NNTensor_Create</span>(size_t deviceID, NN_TensorDesc *tensorDesc)</li></ol></pre></div></div> <p><strong>描述</strong></p> <p>从<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/capi-neuralnetworkruntime-nn-tensordesc">NN_TensorDesc</a>创建一个<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/capi-neuralnetworkruntime-nn-tensor">NN_Tensor</a>实例。</p> <p>该接口使用<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/capi-neural-network-core-h#oh_nntensordesc_getbytesize">OH_NNTensorDesc_GetByteSize</a>计算张量数据的字节数，并为其分配设备内存。设备驱动将直接通过“零拷贝”方式获取张量数据。</p> <p>该接口会将<strong>tensorDesc</strong>复制到<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/capi-neuralnetworkruntime-nn-tensor">NN_Tensor</a>中，因此当<strong>tensorDesc</strong>不再使用时，您应该调用<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/capi-neural-network-core-h#oh_nntensordesc_destroy">OH_NNTensorDesc_Destroy</a>接口销毁它。</p> <p>如果张量形状是动态的，该接口将返回错误码。</p> <p><strong>deviceID</strong>表示所选设备。如果为0，则默认使用设备列表中的第1台设备。</p> <p><strong>必须提供tensorDesc</strong>，如果它是空指针，则返回错误码。</p> <p>当<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/capi-neuralnetworkruntime-nn-tensor">NN_Tensor</a>实例不再使用时，需要调用<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/capi-neural-network-core-h#oh_nntensor_destroy">OH_NNTensor_Destroy</a>销毁它。</p> <p><strong>起始版本：</strong> 11</p> <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>  <div class="tablenoborder"><div class="tbBox"><table class="tableClass2_t"> <tbody><tr class="firstRow"><th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.31.13.1.3.1.1" width="50%">参数项</th> <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.31.13.1.3.1.2" width="50%">描述</th> </tr><tr><td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">size_t deviceID</td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">设备 ID。如果为0，则默认使用当前设备列表中的第1台设备。</td> </tr> <tr><td class="cellrowborder" width="50%"><a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/capi-neuralnetworkruntime-nn-tensordesc">NN_TensorDesc</a> *tensorDesc</td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">指向<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/capi-neuralnetworkruntime-nn-tensordesc">NN_TensorDesc</a>实例的指针。</td> </tr>  </tbody></table></div> </div> <p><strong>返回：</strong></p>  <div class="tablenoborder"><div class="tbBox"><table class="tableClass2_t"> <tbody><tr class="firstRow"><th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.31.15.1.3.1.1" width="50%">类型</th> <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.31.15.1.3.1.2" width="50%">说明</th> </tr><tr><td class="cellrowborder" width="50%"><a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/capi-neuralnetworkruntime-nn-tensor">NN_Tensor</a> *</td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">指向<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/capi-neuralnetworkruntime-nn-tensor">NN_Tensor</a>实例的指针，如果创建失败就返回NULL。</td> </tr>  </tbody></table></div> </div> </div>  <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 1190px;"><h3 id="oh_nntensor_createwithsize" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet">OH_NNTensor_CreateWithSize()<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="oh_nntensor_createwithsize" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3><div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span></div><div _ngcontent-lhx-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-lhx-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-lhx-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-lhx-c106="" class="handle-button expand-button"><div _ngcontent-lhx-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">收起</div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lhx-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-right"><div _ngcontent-lhx-c106="" class="handle-button ai-button"></div><div _ngcontent-lhx-c106="" class="handle-button line-button"><div _ngcontent-lhx-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">自动换行</div></div><div _ngcontent-lhx-c106="" class="handle-button theme-button"><div _ngcontent-lhx-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">深色代码主题</div></div><div _ngcontent-lhx-c106="" class="handle-button copy-button"><div _ngcontent-lhx-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">复制</div></div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lhx-c106="" class="highlight-scroll-div"><pre class="screen prettyprint linenums hljs language-cpp" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li><span class="hljs-function">NN_Tensor *<span class="hljs-title">OH_NNTensor_CreateWithSize</span><span class="hljs-params">(<span class="hljs-type">size_t</span> deviceID, NN_TensorDesc *tensorDesc, <span class="hljs-type">size_t</span> size)</span></span></li></ol></pre></div></div> <p><strong>描述</strong></p> <p>按照指定内存大小和<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/capi-neuralnetworkruntime-nn-tensordesc">NN_TensorDesc</a>创建<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/capi-neuralnetworkruntime-nn-tensor">NN_Tensor</a>实例。</p> <p>该接口使用<strong>size</strong>作为张量数据的字节数，并为其分配设备内存。设备将直接通过“零拷贝”方式获取张量数据。</p> <p>该接口会将<strong>tensorDesc</strong>复制到<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/capi-neuralnetworkruntime-nn-tensor">NN_Tensor</a>中。因此当<strong>tensorDesc</strong>不再使用时，您应该调用<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/capi-neural-network-core-h#oh_nntensordesc_destroy">OH_NNTensorDesc_Destroy</a>接口销毁它。</p> <p><strong>deviceID</strong>表示所选设备ID，如果为0，则使用第1台设备。</p> <p><strong>tensorDesc</strong>必须提供，如果它是空指针，则该接口返回错误码。</p> <p><strong>size</strong>必须不小于<strong>tensorDesc</strong>的数据占用字节数（可由<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/capi-neural-network-core-h#oh_nntensordesc_getbytesize">OH_NNTensorDesc_GetByteSize</a>获取），否则该接口将返回错误码。如果张量形状是动态的，不会检查<strong>size</strong>。</p> <p>当<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/capi-neuralnetworkruntime-nn-tensor">NN_Tensor</a>实例不再使用时，需要调用<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/capi-neural-network-core-h#oh_nntensor_destroy">OH_NNTensor_Destroy</a>销毁它。</p> <p><strong>起始版本：</strong> 11</p> <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>  <div class="tablenoborder"><div class="tbBox"><table class="tableClass2_t"> <tbody><tr class="firstRow"><th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.32.13.1.3.1.1" width="50%">参数项</th> <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.32.13.1.3.1.2" width="50%">描述</th> </tr><tr><td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">size_t deviceID</td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">设备ID。如果为0，则默认使用当前设备列表中的第1台设备。</td> </tr> <tr><td class="cellrowborder" width="50%"><a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/capi-neuralnetworkruntime-nn-tensordesc">NN_TensorDesc</a> *tensorDesc</td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">指向<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/capi-neuralnetworkruntime-nn-tensordesc">NN_TensorDesc</a>实例的指针。</td> </tr> <tr><td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">size_t size</td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">需要分配的张量数据的大小。</td> </tr>  </tbody></table></div> </div> <p><strong>返回：</strong></p>  <div class="tablenoborder"><div class="tbBox"><table class="tableClass2_t"> <tbody><tr class="firstRow"><th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.32.15.1.3.1.1" width="50%">类型</th> <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.32.15.1.3.1.2" width="50%">说明</th> </tr><tr><td class="cellrowborder" width="50%"><a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/capi-neuralnetworkruntime-nn-tensor">NN_Tensor</a> *</td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">指向<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/capi-neuralnetworkruntime-nn-tensor">NN_Tensor</a>实例的指针，如果创建失败就返回NULL。</td> </tr>  </tbody></table></div> </div> </div>  <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 1252px;"><h3 id="oh_nntensor_createwithfd" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet">OH_NNTensor_CreateWithFd()<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="oh_nntensor_createwithfd" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3><div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span></div><div _ngcontent-lhx-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-lhx-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-lhx-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-lhx-c106="" class="handle-button expand-button"><div _ngcontent-lhx-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">收起</div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lhx-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-right"><div _ngcontent-lhx-c106="" class="handle-button ai-button"></div><div _ngcontent-lhx-c106="" class="handle-button line-button"><div _ngcontent-lhx-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">自动换行</div></div><div _ngcontent-lhx-c106="" class="handle-button theme-button"><div _ngcontent-lhx-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">深色代码主题</div></div><div _ngcontent-lhx-c106="" class="handle-button copy-button"><div _ngcontent-lhx-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">复制</div></div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lhx-c106="" class="highlight-scroll-div"><pre class="screen prettyprint linenums hljs language-cpp" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li><span class="hljs-function">NN_Tensor *<span class="hljs-title">OH_NNTensor_CreateWithFd</span><span class="hljs-params">(<span class="hljs-type">size_t</span> deviceID,NN_TensorDesc *tensorDesc,<span class="hljs-type">int</span> fd,<span class="hljs-type">size_t</span> size,<span class="hljs-type">size_t</span> offset)</span></span></li></ol></pre></div></div> <p><strong>描述</strong></p> <p>按照指定共享内存的文件描述符和<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/capi-neuralnetworkruntime-nn-tensordesc">NN_TensorDesc</a>创建<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/capi-neuralnetworkruntime-nn-tensor">NN_Tensor</a>实例。</p> <p>该接口复用文件描述符<strong>fd</strong>对应的共享内存，<strong>fd</strong>可能来自另一个<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/capi-neuralnetworkruntime-nn-tensor">NN_Tensor</a>实例。当调用<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/capi-neural-network-core-h#oh_nntensor_destroy">OH_NNTensor_Destroy</a>接口销毁该接口创建的张量时，不会释放该张量数据的内存。</p> <p>该接口会将<strong>tensorDesc</strong>复制到<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/capi-neuralnetworkruntime-nn-tensor">NN_Tensor</a>中。因此当<strong>tensorDesc</strong>不再使用时，您应该调用<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/capi-neural-network-core-h#oh_nntensordesc_destroy">OH_NNTensorDesc_Destroy</a>接口销毁它。</p> <p><strong>deviceID</strong>表示所选设备。如果为0，则默认使用当前设备列表中的第1台设备。</p> <p>必须提供<strong>tensorDesc</strong>，如果为空指针，则该接口返回错误码。</p> <p>当<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/capi-neuralnetworkruntime-nn-tensor">NN_Tensor</a>实例不再使用时，需要调用<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/capi-neural-network-core-h#oh_nntensor_destroy">OH_NNTensor_Destroy</a>销毁它。</p> <p><strong>起始版本：</strong> 11</p> <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>  <div class="tablenoborder"><div class="tbBox"><table class="tableClass2_t"> <tbody><tr class="firstRow"><th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.33.12.1.3.1.1" href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/capi-neuralnetworkruntime-nn-tensor">NN_Tensor</a>实例的指针，如果创建失败就返回NULL。</td> </tr>  </tbody></table></div> </div> </div>  <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 864px;"><h3 id="oh_nntensor_destroy" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet">OH_NNTensor_Destroy()<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span></div><div _ngcontent-lhx-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-lhx-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-lhx-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-lhx-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">复制</div></div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lhx-c106="" class="highlight-scroll-div"><pre class="screen prettyprint linenums hljs language-scss" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li>OH_NN_ReturnCode <span class="hljs-built_in">OH_NNTensor_Destroy</span>(NN_Tensor **tensor)</li></ol></pre></div></div> <p><strong>描述</strong></p> <p>销毁一个<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/capi-neuralnetworkruntime-nn-tensor">NN_Tensor</a>实例时，需要调用该接口销毁该实例，否则将发生内存泄漏。</p> <p>如果<strong>tensor</strong>或<strong>*tensor</strong>为空指针，则该接口将返回错误码，并且不执行销毁操作。</p> <p><strong>起始版本：</strong> 11</p> <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>  <div class="tablenoborder"><div class="tbBox"><table href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/capi-neuralnetworkruntime-nn-tensor">NN_Tensor</a> **tensor</td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">指向<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/capi-neural-network-runtime-type-h#oh_nn_returncode">OH_NN_ReturnCode</a>。</td> </tr>  </tbody></table></div> </div> </div>  <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 960px;"><h3 id="oh_nntensor_gettensordesc" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet">OH_NNTensor_GetTensorDesc()<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="oh_nntensor_gettensordesc" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3><div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span></div><div _ngcontent-lhx-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-lhx-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-lhx-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-lhx-c106="" class="handle-button expand-button"><div _ngcontent-lhx-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">收起</div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lhx-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-right"><div _ngcontent-lhx-c106="" class="handle-button ai-button"></div><div _ngcontent-lhx-c106="" class="handle-button line-button"><div _ngcontent-lhx-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">自动换行</div></div><div _ngcontent-lhx-c106="" class="handle-button theme-button"><div _ngcontent-lhx-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">深色代码主题</div></div><div _ngcontent-lhx-c106="" class="handle-button copy-button"><div _ngcontent-lhx-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">复制</div></div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lhx-c106="" class="highlight-scroll-div"><pre class="screen prettyprint linenums hljs language-scss" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li>NN_TensorDesc *<span class="hljs-built_in">OH_NNTensor_GetTensorDesc</span>(const NN_Tensor *tensor)</li></ol></pre></div></div> <p><strong>描述</strong></p> <p>获取<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/capi-neuralnetworkruntime-nn-tensor">NN_Tensor</a>的<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/capi-neuralnetworkruntime-nn-tensordesc">NN_TensorDesc</a>实例。</p> <p>调用该接口获取指定<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/capi-neuralnetworkruntime-nn-tensor">NN_Tensor</a>实例的内部<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/capi-neuralnetworkruntime-nn-tensordesc">NN_TensorDesc</a>实例指针。</p> <p>您可以从返回的<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/capi-neuralnetworkruntime-nn-tensordesc">NN_TensorDesc</a>实例中获取各种类型的张量属性，例如名称/数据布局/数据类型/形状等。</p> <p>您不应销毁返回的<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/capi-neuralnetworkruntime-nn-tensordesc">NN_TensorDesc</a>实例，因为它指向了<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/capi-neuralnetworkruntime-nn-tensor">NN_Tensor</a>的内部实例，否则一旦调用<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/capi-neural-network-core-h#oh_nntensor_destroy">OH_NNTensor_Destroy</a>将会发生双重释放的内存崩溃。</p> <p>如果<strong>Tensor</strong>是空指针，则该接口将会返回空指针。</p> <p><strong>起始版本：</strong> 11</p> <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>  <div class="tablenoborder"><div class="tbBox"><table class="tableClass2_t"> <tbody><tr class="firstRow"><th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.35.11.1.3.1.1" width="50%">参数项</th> <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.35.11.1.3.1.2" width="50%">描述</th> </tr><tr><td class="cellrowborder" width="50%"><a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/capi-neuralnetworkruntime-nn-tensor">const NN_Tensor</a> *tensor</td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">指向<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/capi-neuralnetworkruntime-nn-tensor">NN_Tensor</a>实例的指针。</td> </tr>  </tbody></table></div> </div> <p><strong>返回：</strong></p>  <div class="tablenoborder"><div class="tbBox"><table class="tableClass2_t"> <tbody><tr class="firstRow"><th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.35.13.1.3.1.1" width="50%">类型</th> <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.35.13.1.3.1.2" width="50%">说明</th> </tr><tr><td class="cellrowborder" width="50%"><a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/capi-neuralnetworkruntime-nn-tensordesc">NN_TensorDesc</a> *</td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">指向<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/capi-neuralnetworkruntime-nn-tensordesc">NN_TensorDesc</a>实例的指针，如果创建失败就返回NULL。</td> </tr>  </tbody></table></div> </div> </div>  <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 912px;"><h3 id="oh_nntensor_getdatabuffer" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet">OH_NNTensor_GetDataBuffer()<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="oh_nntensor_getdatabuffer" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3><div class="device-list class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-lhx-c106="" class="handle-button expand-button"><div _ngcontent-lhx-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">收起</div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lhx-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-right"><div _ngcontent-lhx-c106="" class="handle-button ai-button"></div><div _ngcontent-lhx-c106="" class="handle-button line-button"><div _ngcontent-lhx-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">自动换行</div></div><div _ngcontent-lhx-c106="" class="handle-button theme-button"><div _ngcontent-lhx-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">深色代码主题</div></div><div _ngcontent-lhx-c106="" class="handle-button copy-button"><div _ngcontent-lhx-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">复制</div></div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lhx-c106="" class="highlight-scroll-div"><pre class="screen prettyprint linenums hljs language-cpp" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li><span class="hljs-function"><span class="hljs-type">void</span> *<span class="hljs-title">OH_NNTensor_GetDataBuffer</span><span class="hljs-params">(<span class="hljs-type">const</span> NN_Tensor *tensor)</span></span></li></ol></pre></div></div> <p><strong>描述</strong></p> <p>获取<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/capi-neuralnetworkruntime-nn-tensor">NN_Tensor</a>数据的内存地址。</p> <p>您可以从张量数据内存读取/写入数据。数据内存是从设备上的共享内存映射的，因此设备驱动可通过这种“零拷贝”方式直接获取张量数据。</p> <p>张量数据仅能使用对应共享内存中的[offset, size)一段，其中offset是共享内存上的偏移量，可以通过<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/capi-neural-network-core-h#oh_nntensor_getoffset">OH_NNTensor_GetOffset</a>获取，而size是共享内存的总大小，可以通过<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/capi-neural-network-core-h#oh_nntensor_getsize">OH_NNTensor_GetSize</a>获取。</p> <p>如果<strong>Tensor</strong>是空指针，则该接口将会返回空指针。</p> <p><strong>起始版本：</strong> 11</p> <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>  <div class="tablenoborder"><div class="tbBox"><table class="tableClass2_t"> <tbody><tr class="firstRow"><th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.36.10.1.3.1.1" width="50%">参数项</th> <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.36.10.1.3.1.2" width="50%">描述</th> </tr><tr><td class="cellrowborder" width="50%"><a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/capi-neuralnetworkruntime-nn-tensor">const NN_Tensor</a> *tensor</td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">指向<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/capi-neuralnetworkruntime-nn-tensor">NN_Tensor</a>实例的指针。</td> </tr>  </tbody></table></div> </div> <p><strong>返回：</strong></p>  <div class="tablenoborder"><div class="tbBox"><table class="tableClass2_t"> <tbody><tr class="firstRow"><th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.36.12.1.3.1.1" width="50%">类型</th> <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.36.12.1.3.1.2" width="50%">说明</th> </tr><tr><td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">void *</td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">指向张量数据内存的指针。如果操作失败，则返回空指针。</td> </tr>  </tbody></table></div> </div> </div>  <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 919px;"><h3 id="oh_nntensor_getfd" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet">OH_NNTensor_GetFd()<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" _ngcontent-lhx-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">深色代码主题</div></div><div _ngcontent-lhx-c106="" class="handle-button copy-button"><div _ngcontent-lhx-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">复制</div></div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lhx-c106="" class="highlight-scroll-div"><pre class="screen prettyprint linenums hljs language-cpp" data-highlighted="yes"><ol <span class="hljs-type">int</span> *fd)</span></span></li></ol></pre></div></div> <p><strong>描述</strong></p> <p>获取<a <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 1015px;"><h3 id="oh_nntensor_getsize" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet">OH_NNTensor_GetSize()<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="oh_nntensor_getsize" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3><div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span></div><div _ngcontent-lhx-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-lhx-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-lhx-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-lhx-c106="" class="handle-button expand-button"><div _ngcontent-lhx-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">收起</div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lhx-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-right"><div _ngcontent-lhx-c106="" class="handle-button ai-button"></div><div _ngcontent-lhx-c106="" class="handle-button line-button"><div _ngcontent-lhx-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">自动换行</div></div><div _ngcontent-lhx-c106="" class="handle-button theme-button"><div _ngcontent-lhx-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">深色代码主题</div></div><div _ngcontent-lhx-c106="" class="handle-button copy-button"><div _ngcontent-lhx-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">复制</div></div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lhx-c106="" class="highlight-scroll-div"><pre class="screen prettyprint linenums hljs language-cpp" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li><span class="hljs-function">OH_NN_ReturnCode <span class="hljs-title">OH_NNTensor_GetSize</span><span class="hljs-params">(<span class="hljs-type">const</span> NN_Tensor *tensor, <span class="hljs-type">size_t</span> *size)</span></span></li></ol></pre></div></div> <p><strong>描述</strong></p> <p>获取<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/capi-neuralnetworkruntime-nn-tensor">NN_Tensor</a>数据所在共享内存的大小。</p> <p><strong>size</strong>与接口<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/capi-neural-network-core-h#oh_nntensor_createwithsize">OH_NNTensor_CreateWithSize</a>和<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/capi-neural-network-core-h#oh_nntensor_createwithfd">OH_NNTensor_CreateWithFd</a>的参数<strong>size</strong>相同，但对于通过<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/capi-neural-network-core-h#oh_nntensor_create">OH_NNTensor_Create</a>创建的张量，<strong>size</strong>等于张量数据实际占用字节数（可由<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/capi-neural-network-core-h#oh_nntensordesc_getbytesize">OH_NNTensorDesc_GetByteSize</a>获取）。</p> <p>张量数据仅能使用文件描述符<strong>fd</strong>对应的共享内存中的[offset, size)一段，其中offset是共享内存上的偏移量，可以通过<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/capi-neural-network-core-h#oh_nntensor_getoffset">OH_NNTensor_GetOffset</a>获取，而size是共享内存的总大小，可以通过<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/capi-neural-network-core-h#oh_nntensor_getsize">OH_NNTensor_GetSize</a>获取。</p> <p>如果<strong>tensor</strong>或<strong>size</strong>为空指针，该接口将返回错误。</p> <p><strong>起始版本：</strong> 11</p> <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>  <div class="tablenoborder"><div class="tbBox"><table href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/capi-neuralnetworkruntime-nn-tensor">NN_Tensor</a>实例的指针。</td> </tr> <tr><td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">size_t *size</td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">返回的数据所在共享内存的大小。</td> </tr>  </tbody></table></div> </div> <p><strong>返回：</strong></p>  <div class="tablenoborder"><div class="tbBox"><table class="tableClass2_t"> <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 864px;"><h3 id="oh_nnexecutor_construct" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet">OH_NNExecutor_Construct()<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="oh_nnexecutor_construct" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3><div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span></div><div _ngcontent-lhx-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-lhx-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-lhx-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-lhx-c106="" class="handle-button expand-button"><div _ngcontent-lhx-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">收起</div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lhx-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-right"><div _ngcontent-lhx-c106="" class="handle-button ai-button"></div><div _ngcontent-lhx-c106="" class="handle-button line-button"><div _ngcontent-lhx-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">自动换行</div></div><div _ngcontent-lhx-c106="" class="handle-button theme-button"><div _ngcontent-lhx-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">深色代码主题</div></div><div _ngcontent-lhx-c106="" class="handle-button copy-button"><div _ngcontent-lhx-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">复制</div></div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lhx-c106="" class="highlight-scroll-div"><pre class="screen prettyprint linenums hljs language-scss" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li>OH_NNExecutor *<span class="hljs-built_in">OH_NNExecutor_Construct</span>(OH_NNCompilation *compilation)</li></ol></pre></div></div> <p><strong>描述</strong></p> <p>创建<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/capi-neuralnetworkruntime-oh-nnexecutor">OH_NNExecutor</a>执行器实例。</p> <p>该接口接受一个<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/capi-neuralnetworkruntime-oh-nncompilation">OH_NNCompilation</a>实例，构造一个与硬件关联的模型推理执行器。通过<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/capi-neural-network-runtime-h#oh_nnexecutor_setinput">OH_NNExecutor_SetInput</a>设置模型输入数据，设置输入数据后，调用<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/capi-neural-network-runtime-h#oh_nnexecutor_run">OH_NNExecutor_Run</a>接口执行推理，最后通过<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/capi-neural-network-runtime-h#oh_nnexecutor_setoutput">OH_NNExecutor_SetOutput</a>获取计算结果。 通过<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/capi-neuralnetworkruntime-oh-nncompilation">OH_NNCompilation</a>实例创建一个<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/capi-neuralnetworkruntime-oh-nnexecutor">OH_NNExecutor</a>实例后，如果不再使用<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/capi-neuralnetworkruntime-oh-nncompilation">OH_NNCompilation</a>实例创建其他<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/capi-neuralnetworkruntime-oh-nnexecutor">OH_NNExecutor</a>实例，就可以销毁<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/capi-neuralnetworkruntime-oh-nncompilation">OH_NNCompilation</a>实例了。</p> <p><strong>起始版本：</strong> 9</p> <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 1293px;"><h3 id="oh_nnexecutor_getoutputshape" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet">OH_NNExecutor_GetOutputShape()<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="oh_nnexecutor_getoutputshape" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3><div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span></div><div _ngcontent-lhx-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-lhx-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-lhx-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-lhx-c106="" class="handle-button expand-button"><div _ngcontent-lhx-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">收起</div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lhx-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-right"><div _ngcontent-lhx-c106="" class="handle-button ai-button"></div><div _ngcontent-lhx-c106="" class="handle-button line-button"><div _ngcontent-lhx-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">自动换行</div></div><div _ngcontent-lhx-c106="" class="handle-button theme-button"><div _ngcontent-lhx-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">深色代码主题</div></div><div _ngcontent-lhx-c106="" class="handle-button copy-button"><div _ngcontent-lhx-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">复制</div></div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lhx-c106="" class="highlight-scroll-div"><pre class="screen prettyprint linenums hljs language-cpp" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li><span class="hljs-function">OH_NN_ReturnCode <span class="hljs-title">OH_NNExecutor_GetOutputShape</span><span class="hljs-params">(OH_NNExecutor *executor,<span class="hljs-type">uint32_t</span> outputIndex,<span class="hljs-type">int32_t</span> **shape,<span class="hljs-type">uint32_t</span> *shapeLength)</span></span></li></ol></pre></div></div> <p><strong>描述</strong></p> <p>获取输出张量的维度信息。</p> <p>调用<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/capi-neural-network-runtime-h#oh_nnexecutor_run">OH_NNExecutor_Run</a>完成单次推理后，该接口获取指定输出的维度信息和维数。在动态形状输入、输出的场景中常用。</p> <p>如果索引值<strong>outputIndex</strong>达到或超过输出张量的数量，接口将返回错误。输出张量的数量可以通过<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/capi-neural-network-core-h#oh_nnexecutor_getoutputcount">OH_NNExecutor_GetOutputCount</a>获取。</p> <p>作为输出参数，<strong>*shape</strong>不能为空指针，否则会返回错误。例如您应该定义int32_t* tensorShape = NULL，然后将&amp;tensorShape作为参数传入。</p> <p>您无需释放<strong>shape</strong>的内存，它会随<strong>executor</strong>一起被释放。</p> <p><strong>起始版本：</strong> 9</p> <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>  <div class="tablenoborder"><div class="tbBox"><table class="tableClass2_t"> <tbody><tr class="firstRow"><th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.41.11.1.3.1.1" width="50%">参数项</th> <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.41.11.1.3.1.2" width="50%">描述</th> </tr><tr><td class="cellrowborder" width="50%"><a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/capi-neuralnetworkruntime-oh-nnexecutor">OH_NNExecutor</a> *executor</td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">指向<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/capi-neuralnetworkruntime-oh-nnexecutor">OH_NNExecutor</a>实例的指针。</td> </tr> <tr><td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">uint32_t outputIndex</td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">输出的索引值，与调用<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/capi-neural-network-runtime-h#oh_nnmodel_specifyinputsandoutputs">OH_NNModel_SpecifyInputsAndOutputs</a>时输出数据的顺序一致。假设调用<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/capi-neural-network-runtime-h#oh_nnmodel_specifyinputsandoutputs">OH_NNModel_SpecifyInputsAndOutputs</a>时，outputIndices为{4, 6, 8}，则在获取输出张量维度信息时，三个输出的索引值分别为{0, 1, 2}。</td> </tr> <tr><td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">int32_t **shape</td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">指向int32_t数组的指针，数组中的每个元素值，是输出张量在每个维度上的长度。</td> </tr> <tr><td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">uint32_t *shapeLength</td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">uint32_t类型的指针，返回输出的维数。</td> </tr>  </tbody></table></div> </div> <p><strong>返回：</strong></p>  <div class="tablenoborder"><div class="tbBox"><table class="tableClass2_t"> <tbody><tr class="firstRow"><th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.41.13.1.3.1.1" width="50%">类型</th> <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.41.13.1.3.1.2" width="50%">说明</th> </tr><tr><td class="cellrowborder" width="50%"><a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/capi-neural-network-runtime-type-h#oh_nn_returncode">OH_NN_ReturnCode</a></td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">函数执行的结果状态。执行成功返回OH_NN_SUCCESS；失败返回具体错误码，具体失败错误码可参考<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/capi-neural-network-runtime-type-h#oh_nn_returncode">OH_NN_ReturnCode</a>。</td> </tr>  </tbody></table></div> </div> </div> <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 871px;"><h3 id="oh_nnexecutor_createoutputtensordesc" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet">OH_NNExecutor_CreateOutputTensorDesc()<i <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 1348px;"><h3 id="oh_nnexecutor_getinputdimrange" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet">OH_NNExecutor_GetInputDimRange()<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="oh_nnexecutor_getinputdimrange" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3><div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span></div><div _ngcontent-lhx-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-lhx-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-lhx-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-lhx-c106="" class="handle-button expand-button"><div _ngcontent-lhx-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">收起</div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lhx-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-right"><div _ngcontent-lhx-c106="" class="handle-button ai-button"></div><div _ngcontent-lhx-c106="" class="handle-button line-button"><div _ngcontent-lhx-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">自动换行</div></div><div _ngcontent-lhx-c106="" class="handle-button theme-button"><div _ngcontent-lhx-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">深色代码主题</div></div><div _ngcontent-lhx-c106="" class="handle-button copy-button"><div _ngcontent-lhx-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">复制</div></div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lhx-c106="" class="highlight-scroll-div"><pre class="screen prettyprint linenums hljs language-cpp" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li><span class="hljs-function">OH_NN_ReturnCode <span class="hljs-title">OH_NNExecutor_GetInputDimRange</span><span class="hljs-params">(<span class="hljs-type">const</span> OH_NNExecutor *executor,<span class="hljs-type">size_t</span> index,<span class="hljs-type">size_t</span> **minInputDims,<span class="hljs-type">size_t</span> **maxInputDims,<span class="hljs-type">size_t</span> *shapeLength)</span></span></li></ol></pre></div></div> <p><strong>描述</strong></p> <p>获取所有输入张量的维度范围。</p> <p>当输入张量具有动态形状时，它在不同硬件上支持的维度范围可能是不同的，可以通过该接口获取当前设备上支持的维度范围。<strong>*minInputDims</strong>保存了指定输入张量的最小维度（维度数与形状匹配），而<strong>*maxInputDims</strong>则保存了最大维度。</p> <p>例如，一个输入张量具有动态形状 [-1, -1, -1, 3]，那么当前设备上它的<strong>*minInputDims</strong>可以是[1, 10, 10, 3]，而<strong>*maxInputDims</strong>可以是[100, 1024, 1024, 3]。</p> <p>如果索引值<strong>index</strong>达到或超过输入张量的数量，接口将返回错误。输入张量的数量可以通过<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/capi-neural-network-core-h#oh_nnexecutor_getinputcount">OH_NNExecutor_GetInputCount</a>获取。</p> <p>作为输出参数，<strong>*minInputDims</strong>和<strong>*maxInputDims</strong>不能为空指针，否则会返回错误。例如您应该定义int32_t* minInDims = NULL，然后将&amp;minInDims作为参数传入。</p> <p>您无需释放<strong>*minInputDims</strong>和<strong>*maxInputDims</strong>的内存，它会随<strong>executor</strong>一起被释放。</p> <p><strong>起始版本：</strong> 11</p> <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>  <div class="tablenoborder"><div class="tbBox"><table class="tableClass2_t"> <tbody><tr class="firstRow"><th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.47.12.1.3.1.1" width="50%">参数项</th> <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.47.12.1.3.1.2" width="50%">描述</th> </tr><tr><td class="cellrowborder" width="50%"><a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/capi-neuralnetworkruntime-oh-nnexecutor">const OH_NNExecutor</a> *executor</td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">指向<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/capi-neuralnetworkruntime-oh-nnexecutor">OH_NNExecutor</a>实例的指针。</td> </tr> <tr><td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">size_t index</td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">输入张量的索引值。</td> </tr> <tr><td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">size_t **minInputDims</td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">返回的数组的指针，保存了指定输入张量的最小维度（维度数与形状匹配）。</td> </tr> <tr><td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">size_t **maxInputDims</td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">返回的数组的指针，保存了指定输入张量的最大维度（维度数与形状匹配）。</td> </tr> <tr><td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">size_t *shapeLength</td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">返回的输入张量的维度数量，与形状一致。</td> </tr>  </tbody></table></div> </div> <p><strong>返回：</strong></p>  <div class="tablenoborder"><div class="tbBox"><table class="tableClass2_t"> <tbody><tr class="firstRow"><th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.47.14.1.3.1.1" width="50%">类型</th> <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.47.14.1.3.1.2" width="50%">说明</th> </tr><tr><td class="cellrowborder" width="50%"><a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/capi-neural-network-runtime-type-h#oh_nn_returncode">OH_NN_ReturnCode</a></td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">函数执行的结果状态。执行成功返回OH_NN_SUCCESS；失败返回具体错误码，具体失败错误码可参考<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/capi-neural-network-runtime-type-h#oh_nn_returncode">OH_NN_ReturnCode</a>。</td> </tr>  </tbody></table></div> </div> </div>  <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 871px;"><h3 id="oh_nnexecutor_setonrundone" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet">OH_NNExecutor_SetOnRunDone()<i class="anchor-icon <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 871px;"><h3 id="oh_nnexecutor_setonservicedied" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet">OH_NNExecutor_SetOnServiceDied()<i class="anchor-icon width="50%"><a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/capi-neural-network-runtime-type-h#oh_nn_returncode">OH_NN_ReturnCode</a></td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">函数执行的结果状态。执行成功返回OH_NN_SUCCESS；失败返回具体错误码，具体失败错误码可参考<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/capi-neural-network-runtime-type-h#oh_nn_returncode">OH_NN_ReturnCode</a>。</td> </tr>  </tbody></table></div> </div> </div>  <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 1156px;"><h3 id="oh_nnexecutor_runsync" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet">OH_NNExecutor_RunSync()<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="oh_nnexecutor_runsync" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3><div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span></div><div _ngcontent-lhx-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-lhx-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-lhx-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-lhx-c106="" class="handle-button expand-button"><div _ngcontent-lhx-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">收起</div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lhx-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-right"><div _ngcontent-lhx-c106="" class="handle-button ai-button"></div><div _ngcontent-lhx-c106="" class="handle-button line-button"><div _ngcontent-lhx-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">自动换行</div></div><div _ngcontent-lhx-c106="" class="handle-button theme-button"><div _ngcontent-lhx-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">深色代码主题</div></div><div _ngcontent-lhx-c106="" class="handle-button copy-button"><div _ngcontent-lhx-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">复制</div></div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lhx-c106="" class="highlight-scroll-div"><pre class="screen prettyprint linenums hljs language-cpp" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li><span class="hljs-function">OH_NN_ReturnCode <span class="hljs-title">OH_NNExecutor_RunSync</span><span class="hljs-params">(OH_NNExecutor *executor,NN_Tensor *inputTensor[],<span class="hljs-type">size_t</span> inputCount,NN_Tensor *outputTensor[],<span class="hljs-type">size_t</span> outputCount)</span></span></li></ol></pre></div></div> <p><strong>描述</strong></p> <p>执行同步推理。</p> <p>需要先通过<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/capi-neural-network-core-h#oh_nntensor_create">OH_NNTensor_Create</a>、<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/capi-neural-network-core-h#oh_nntensor_createwithsize">OH_NNTensor_CreateWithSize</a>或<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/capi-neural-network-core-h#oh_nntensor_createwithfd">OH_NNTensor_CreateWithFd</a>接口创建输入和输出张量。然后由<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/capi-neural-network-core-h#oh_nntensor_getdatabuffer">OH_NNTensor_GetDataBuffer</a>获取张量数据指针并向其拷贝输入数据。执行器会通过执行推理产生推理结果，并将结果写入输出张量中。</p> <p>如果输出张量具有动态形状，可以通过<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/capi-neural-network-core-h#oh_nnexecutor_getoutputshape">OH_NNExecutor_GetOutputShape</a>接口获取输出张量的实际形状。或者通过<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/capi-neural-network-core-h#oh_nntensor_gettensordesc">OH_NNTensor_GetTensorDesc</a>接口从输入张量中获取张量描述，然后通过<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/capi-neural-network-core-h#oh_nntensordesc_getshape">OH_NNTensorDesc_GetShape</a>接口获取实际形状。</p> <p><strong>起始版本：</strong> 11</p> <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>  <div class="tablenoborder"><div class="tbBox"><table class="tableClass2_t"> <tbody><tr class="firstRow"><th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.50.9.1.3.1.1" width="50%">参数项</th> <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.50.9.1.3.1.2" width="50%">描述</th> </tr><tr><td class="cellrowborder" width="50%"><a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/capi-neuralnetworkruntime-oh-nnexecutor">OH_NNExecutor</a> *executor</td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">指向<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/capi-neuralnetworkruntime-oh-nnexecutor">OH_NNExecutor</a>实例的指针。</td> </tr> <tr><td class="cellrowborder" width="50%"><a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/capi-neuralnetworkruntime-nn-tensor">NN_Tensor</a> *inputTensor[]</td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">输入张量的数组。</td> </tr> <tr><td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">size_t inputCount</td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">输入张量的数量。</td> </tr> <tr><td class="cellrowborder" width="50%"><a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/capi-neuralnetworkruntime-nn-tensor">NN_Tensor</a> *outputTensor[]</td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">输出张量的数组。</td> </tr> <tr><td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">size_t outputCount</td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">输出张量的数量。</td> </tr>  </tbody></table></div> </div> <p><strong>返回：</strong></p>  <div class="tablenoborder"><div class="tbBox"><table class="tableClass2_t"> <tbody><tr class="firstRow"><th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.50.11.1.3.1.1" width="50%">类型</th> <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.50.11.1.3.1.2" width="50%">说明</th> </tr><tr><td class="cellrowborder" width="50%"><a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/capi-neural-network-runtime-type-h#oh_nn_returncode">OH_NN_ReturnCode</a></td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">函数执行的结果状态。执行成功返回OH_NN_SUCCESS；失败返回具体错误码，具体失败错误码可参考<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/capi-neural-network-runtime-type-h#oh_nn_returncode">OH_NN_ReturnCode</a>。</td> </tr>  </tbody></table></div> </div> </div>  <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 1530px;"><h3 id="oh_nnexecutor_runasync" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet">OH_NNExecutor_RunAsync()<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="oh_nnexecutor_runasync" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3><div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span></div><div _ngcontent-lhx-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-lhx-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-lhx-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-lhx-c106="" class="handle-button expand-button"><div _ngcontent-lhx-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">收起</div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lhx-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-right"><div _ngcontent-lhx-c106="" class="handle-button ai-button"></div><div _ngcontent-lhx-c106="" class="handle-button line-button"><div _ngcontent-lhx-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">自动换行</div></div><div _ngcontent-lhx-c106="" class="handle-button theme-button"><div _ngcontent-lhx-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">深色代码主题</div></div><div _ngcontent-lhx-c106="" class="handle-button copy-button"><div _ngcontent-lhx-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">复制</div></div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lhx-c106="" class="highlight-scroll-div"><pre class="screen prettyprint linenums hljs language-cpp" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li><span class="hljs-function">OH_NN_ReturnCode <span class="hljs-title">OH_NNExecutor_RunAsync</span><span class="hljs-params">(OH_NNExecutor *executor,NN_Tensor *inputTensor[],<span class="hljs-type">size_t</span> inputCount,NN_Tensor *outputTensor[],<span class="hljs-type">size_t</span> outputCount,<span class="hljs-type">int32_t</span> timeout,<span class="hljs-type">void</span> *userData)</span></span></li></ol></pre></div></div> <p><strong>描述</strong></p> <p>执行异步推理。</p> <p>需要先通过<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/capi-neural-network-core-h#oh_nntensor_create">OH_NNTensor_Create</a>、<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/capi-neural-network-core-h#oh_nntensor_createwithsize">OH_NNTensor_CreateWithSize</a>或<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/capi-neural-network-core-h#oh_nntensor_createwithfd">OH_NNTensor_CreateWithFd</a>接口创建输入和输出张量。然后由<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/capi-neural-network-core-h#oh_nntensor_getdatabuffer">OH_NNTensor_GetDataBuffer</a>获取张量数据指针并向其拷贝输入数据。执行器会通过执行推理产生推理结果，并将结果写入输出张量中。</p> <p>如果输出张量具有动态形状，可以通过<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/capi-neural-network-core-h#oh_nnexecutor_getoutputshape">OH_NNExecutor_GetOutputShape</a>接口获取输出张量的实际形状。或者通过<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/capi-neural-network-core-h#oh_nntensor_gettensordesc">OH_NNTensor_GetTensorDesc</a>接口从输入张量中获取张量描述，然后通过<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/capi-neural-network-core-h#oh_nntensordesc_getshape">OH_NNTensorDesc_GetShape</a>接口获取实际形状。</p> <p>该接口是非阻塞式的，调用后会立刻返回，而推理结果、执行返回状态可以通过回调函数<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/capi-neural-network-runtime-type-h#nn_onrundone">NN_OnRunDone</a>来获取。如果设备驱动服务在执行过程中异常终止，可以通过回调函数<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/capi-neural-network-runtime-type-h#nn_onservicedied">NN_OnServiceDied</a>来处理。</p> <p>可以通过接口<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/capi-neural-network-core-h#oh_nnexecutor_setonrundone">OH_NNExecutor_SetOnRunDone</a>和<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/capi-neural-network-core-h#oh_nnexecutor_setonservicedied">OH_NNExecutor_SetOnServiceDied</a>设置回调函数<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/capi-neural-network-runtime-type-h#nn_onrundone">NN_OnRunDone</a>和<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/capi-neural-network-runtime-type-h#nn_onservicedied">NN_OnServiceDied</a>。</p> <p>如果推理时长超过了timeout，会立刻终止推理，回调函数<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/capi-neural-network-runtime-type-h#nn_onrundone">NN_OnRunDone</a>的errCode参数会返回<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/capi-neural-network-runtime-type-h#oh_nn_returncode">OH_NN_TIMEOUT</a>错误。</p> <p>userData是区分不同次异步执行的标识符，会作为回调函数的第一个参数返回，您可以使用能够区分不同次执行的任意数据作为标识符。</p> <p><strong>起始版本：</strong> 11</p> <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>  <div class="tablenoborder"><div class="tbBox"><table class="tableClass2_t"> <tbody><tr class="firstRow"><th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.51.13.1.3.1.1" width="50%">参数项</th> <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.51.13.1.3.1.2" width="50%">描述</th> </tr><tr><td class="cellrowborder" width="50%"><a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/capi-neuralnetworkruntime-oh-nnexecutor">OH_NNExecutor</a> *executor</td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">指向<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/capi-neuralnetworkruntime-oh-nnexecutor">OH_NNExecutor</a>实例的指针。</td> </tr> <tr><td class="cellrowborder" width="50%"><a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/capi-neuralnetworkruntime-nn-tensor">NN_Tensor</a> *inputTensor[]</td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">输入张量的数组。</td> </tr> <tr><td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">size_t inputCount</td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">输入张量的数量。</td> </tr> <tr><td class="cellrowborder" width="50%"><a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/capi-neuralnetworkruntime-nn-tensor">NN_Tensor</a> *outputTensor[]</td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">输出张量的数组。</td> </tr> <tr><td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">size_t outputCount</td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">输出张量的数量。</td> </tr> <tr><td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">int32_t timeout</td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">异步推理的超时时间（单位ms），例如1000。</td> </tr> <tr><td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">void *userData</td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">异步执行的标识符。</td> </tr>  </tbody></table></div> </div> <p><strong>返回：</strong></p>  <div class="tablenoborder"><div class="tbBox"><table class="tableClass2_t"> <tbody><tr class="firstRow"><th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.51.15.1.3.1.1" width="50%">类型</th> <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.51.15.1.3.1.2" width="50%">说明</th> </tr><tr><td class="cellrowborder" width="50%"><a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/capi-neural-network-runtime-type-h#oh_nn_returncode">OH_NN_ReturnCode</a></td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">函数执行的结果状态。执行成功返回OH_NN_SUCCESS；失败返回具体错误码，具体失败错误码可参考<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/capi-neural-network-runtime-type-h#oh_nn_returncode">OH_NN_ReturnCode</a>。</td> </tr>  </tbody></table></div> </div> </div>  <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 967px;"><h3 id="oh_nndevice_getalldevicesid" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet">OH_NNDevice_GetAllDevicesID()<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="oh_nndevice_getalldevicesid" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3><div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span></div><div _ngcontent-lhx-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-lhx-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-lhx-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-lhx-c106="" class="handle-button expand-button"><div _ngcontent-lhx-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">收起</div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lhx-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-right"><div _ngcontent-lhx-c106="" class="handle-button ai-button"></div><div _ngcontent-lhx-c106="" class="handle-button line-button"><div _ngcontent-lhx-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">自动换行</div></div><div _ngcontent-lhx-c106="" class="handle-button theme-button"><div _ngcontent-lhx-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">深色代码主题</div></div><div _ngcontent-lhx-c106="" class="handle-button copy-button"><div _ngcontent-lhx-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">复制</div></div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lhx-c106="" class="highlight-scroll-div"><pre class="screen prettyprint linenums hljs language-cpp" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li><span class="hljs-function">OH_NN_ReturnCode <span class="hljs-title">OH_NNDevice_GetAllDevicesID</span><span class="hljs-params">(<span class="hljs-type">const</span> <span class="hljs-type">size_t</span> **allDevicesID, <span class="hljs-type">uint32_t</span> *deviceCount)</span></span></li></ol></pre></div></div> <p><strong>描述</strong></p> <p>获取对接到Neural Network Runtime的硬件ID。</p> <p>每个硬件存在唯一且固定的ID，该接口通过uint32_t数组返回当前设备上已经对接的硬件ID。</p> <p>硬件ID通过size_t数组返回，数组的每个元素是单个硬件的ID值。数组内存由内部进行管理，在下次调用该接口前，数据指针将一直有效。</p> <p><strong>起始版本：</strong> 9</p> <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>  <div class="tablenoborder"><div class="tbBox"><table class="tableClass2_t"> <tbody><tr class="firstRow"><th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.52.9.1.3.1.1" width="50%">参数项</th> <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.52.9.1.3.1.2" width="50%">描述</th> </tr><tr><td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">const size_t **allDevicesID</td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">指向size_t数组的指针。要求传入的*allDevicesID为空指针，否则将返回错误码<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/capi-neural-network-runtime-type-h#oh_nn_returncode">OH_NN_INVALID_PARAMETER</a>。</td> </tr> <tr><td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">uint32_t *deviceCount</td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">uint32_t类型的指针，用于返回*allDevicesID的长度。</td> </tr>  </tbody></table></div> </div> <p><strong>返回：</strong></p>  <div class="tablenoborder"><div class="tbBox"><table class="tableClass2_t"> <tbody><tr class="firstRow"><th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.52.11.1.3.1.1" width="50%">类型</th> <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.52.11.1.3.1.2" width="50%">说明</th> </tr><tr><td class="cellrowborder" width="50%"><a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/capi-neural-network-runtime-type-h#oh_nn_returncode">OH_NN_ReturnCode</a></td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">函数执行的结果状态。执行成功返回OH_NN_SUCCESS；失败返回具体错误码，具体失败错误码可参考<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/capi-neural-network-runtime-type-h#oh_nn_returncode">OH_NN_ReturnCode</a>。</td> </tr>  </tbody></table></div> </div> </div>  <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 943px;"><h3 id="oh_nndevice_getname" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet">OH_NNDevice_GetName()<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="oh_nndevice_getname" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3><div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span></div><div _ngcontent-lhx-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-lhx-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-lhx-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-lhx-c106="" class="handle-button expand-button"><div _ngcontent-lhx-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">收起</div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lhx-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-right"><div _ngcontent-lhx-c106="" class="handle-button ai-button"></div><div _ngcontent-lhx-c106="" class="handle-button line-button"><div _ngcontent-lhx-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">自动换行</div></div><div _ngcontent-lhx-c106="" class="handle-button theme-button"><div _ngcontent-lhx-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">深色代码主题</div></div><div _ngcontent-lhx-c106="" class="handle-button copy-button"><div _ngcontent-lhx-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">复制</div></div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lhx-c106="" class="highlight-scroll-div"><pre class="screen prettyprint linenums hljs language-cpp" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li><span class="hljs-function">OH_NN_ReturnCode <span class="hljs-title">OH_NNDevice_GetName</span><span class="hljs-params">(<span class="hljs-type">size_t</span> deviceID, <span class="hljs-type">const</span> <span class="hljs-type">char</span> **name)</span></span></li></ol></pre></div></div> <p><strong>描述</strong></p> <p>获取指定硬件的名称。</p> <p>通过deviceID指定计算硬件，获取硬件的名称。硬件ID需要调用<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/capi-neural-network-core-h#oh_nndevice_getalldevicesid">OH_NNDevice_GetAllDevicesID</a>获取。如果deviceID是0，那么会默认使用设备列表中的第一个设备。 *name是一个C风格的字符串，以'\0'作为结束符。*name必须是一个空指针，否则接口会返回<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/capi-neural-network-runtime-type-h#oh_nn_returncode">OH_NN_INVALID_PARAMETER</a>错误。例如您应该定义char* deviceName = NULL，然后将&amp;deviceName作为参数传入。</p> <p><strong>起始版本：</strong> 9</p> <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>  <div class="tablenoborder"><div class="tbBox"><table class="tableClass2_t"> <tbody><tr class="firstRow"><th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.53.8.1.3.1.1" width="50%">参数项</th> <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.53.8.1.3.1.2" width="50%">描述</th> </tr><tr><td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">size_t deviceID</td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">指定硬件ID。如果deviceID是0，那么会默认使用设备列表中的第一个设备。</td> </tr> <tr><td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">const char **name</td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">指向char数组的指针，保存返回的硬件名称。</td> </tr>  </tbody></table></div> </div> <p><strong>返回：</strong></p>  <div class="tablenoborder"><div class="tbBox"><table class="tableClass2_t"> <tbody><tr class="firstRow"><th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.53.10.1.3.1.1" width="50%">类型</th> <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.53.10.1.3.1.2" width="50%">说明</th> </tr><tr><td class="cellrowborder" width="50%"><a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/capi-neural-network-runtime-type-h#oh_nn_returncode">OH_NN_ReturnCode</a></td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">函数执行的结果状态。执行成功返回OH_NN_SUCCESS；失败返回具体错误码，具体失败错误码可参考<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/capi-neural-network-runtime-type-h#oh_nn_returncode">OH_NN_ReturnCode</a>。</td> </tr>  </tbody></table></div> </div> </div>  <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 1087px;"><h3 id="oh_nndevice_gettype" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet">OH_NNDevice_GetType()<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="oh_nndevice_gettype" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3><div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span></div><div _ngcontent-lhx-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-lhx-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-lhx-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-lhx-c106="" class="handle-button expand-button"><div _ngcontent-lhx-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">收起</div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lhx-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-right"><div _ngcontent-lhx-c106="" class="handle-button ai-button"></div><div _ngcontent-lhx-c106="" class="handle-button line-button"><div _ngcontent-lhx-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">自动换行</div></div><div _ngcontent-lhx-c106="" class="handle-button theme-button"><div _ngcontent-lhx-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">深色代码主题</div></div><div _ngcontent-lhx-c106="" class="handle-button copy-button"><div _ngcontent-lhx-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">复制</div></div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lhx-c106="" class="highlight-scroll-div"><pre class="screen prettyprint linenums hljs language-scss" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li>OH_NN_ReturnCode <span class="hljs-built_in">OH_NNDevice_GetType</span>(size_t deviceID, OH_NN_DeviceType *deviceType)</li></ol></pre></div></div> <p><strong>描述</strong></p> <p>获取指定硬件的类别信息。</p> <p>通过deviceID指定计算硬件，获取硬件的类别。如果deviceID是0，那么会默认使用设备列表中的第一个设备。目前支持的设备类型有：</p> <ul><li><p>CPU设备：OH_NN_CPU</p>  </li><li><p>GPU设备：OH_NN_GPU</p>  </li><li><p>机器学习专用加速器：OH_NN_ACCELERATOR</p>  </li><li><p>不属于以上类型的其他硬件类型：OH_NN_OTHERS</p>  </li></ul> <p><strong>起始版本：</strong> 9</p> <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>  <div class="tablenoborder"><div class="tbBox"><table class="tableClass2_t"> <tbody><tr class="firstRow"><th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.54.9.1.3.1.1" width="50%">参数项</th> <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.54.9.1.3.1.2" width="50%">描述</th> </tr><tr><td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">size_t deviceID</td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">指定硬件ID。如果deviceID是0，那么会默认使用设备列表中的第一个设备。</td> </tr> <tr><td class="cellrowborder" width="50%"><a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/capi-neural-network-runtime-type-h#oh_nn_devicetype">OH_NN_DeviceType</a> *deviceType</td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">指向<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/capi-neural-network-runtime-type-h#oh_nn_devicetype">OH_NN_DeviceType</a>实例的指针，返回硬件的类别信息。</td> </tr>  </tbody></table></div> </div> <p><strong>返回：</strong></p>  <div class="tablenoborder"><div class="tbBox"><table class="tableClass2_t"> <tbody><tr class="firstRow"><th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.54.11.1.3.1.1" width="50%">类型</th> <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.54.11.1.3.1.2" width="50%">说明</th> </tr><tr><td class="cellrowborder" width="50%"><a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/capi-neural-network-runtime-type-h#oh_nn_returncode">OH_NN_ReturnCode</a></td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">函数执行的结果状态。执行成功返回OH_NN_SUCCESS；失败返回具体错误码，具体失败错误码可参考<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/capi-neural-network-runtime-type-h#oh_nn_returncode">OH_NN_ReturnCode</a>。</td> </tr>  </tbody></table></div> </div> </div>
